\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__nmf_8py_source_l00159}00159\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ res\ =\ np.dot(X\_data,\ np.log(div))}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__nmf_8py_source_l00160}00160\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ add\ full\ np.sum(np.dot(W,\ H))\ -\/\ np.sum(X)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__nmf_8py_source_l00161}00161\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ res\ +=\ sum\_WH\ -\/\ X\_data.sum()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__nmf_8py_source_l00162}00162\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__nmf_8py_source_l00163}00163\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ Itakura-\/Saito\ divergence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__nmf_8py_source_l00164}00164\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif}\ beta\ ==\ 0:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__nmf_8py_source_l00165}00165\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ div\ =\ X\_data\ /\ WH\_data}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__nmf_8py_source_l00166}00166\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ res\ =\ np.sum(div)\ -\/\ np.prod(X.shape)\ -\/\ np.sum(np.log(div))}
